Inkscape's primary vector graphics format is Scalable Vector Graphics (SVG), however many other formats can be imported and exported.\r\n\r\nInkscape can render primitive vector shapes (e.g. rectangles, ellipses, polygons, arcs, spirals, stars and 3D boxes) and text. Embedding and optional tracing of raster graphics is also supported, enabling the editor to create vector graphics from photos and other raster sources.
